Let me consider `e4f5`: bishop to f5 is check! King on g4, bishop on f5 attacks g4 diagonally. The king's escape squares: g4 can go to f4? No, my rook covers f3 area. After Bf5+, king must move. King to h3, then my rook on f3 controls...
